# 118\n
{BL Cotton Titus D xviii, fols. 14r-105r: Ancrene Riwle}\n
C13a2(1240-50)\n
370 349 E\n
{=S Cheshire=}\n
{=Sample tagged - fols. 14r-40r. The texts in this MS are all in one\n
hand but in different types of language. Ancrene Riwle is in two basic\n
types: T1, a homogeneous North-West Midland type of language,\n
represented by this sample; and T2, a mixture of T1 and something more\n
southerly, for which see text no. 119. Apart from the stretches\n
noticed as T2 all the rest of AR is in T1. The other texts (each\n
tagged separately) are in mixed language similar to T2, apart from the\n
Wohunge of ure Lauerd for which see text no. 122 (tituswoht.tag)=}\n
{=Script - Textura semi-quadrata=}\n
{=Status - MS punctuation done; tagging notes and textual notes up to date=}\n
{=Begins imperfectly=}\n
{~f14ra~}\n
